\begin{model}

\begin{problem}
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œ$\triangle ABC$ä¸­ï¼Œ$AB=AC$ï¼Œ$\angle ADE=\angle B,\angle ADF=\angle C,EF$äº¤$AD$äº$G$. \\

\begin{problem}
    å¦‚å›¾(1)ï¼Œ$\triangle ABC$ä¸­ï¼Œ$CA^2=CDÂ·CB.$ \\

\begin{model}
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œ$\angle ABD=\angle ACD$ï¼Œåˆ™$A,B,C,D$å››ç‚¹å…±åœ†ï¼Œå›¾ä¸­æœ‰è‹¥å¹²å¯¹ç›¸ä¼¼ä¸‰è§’å½¢ï¼Œå¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š\\
    (1)$\triangle AOB \sim \triangle DOC (\angle ABO=\angle DCO, \angle AOB=\angle DOC)$ \\
    (2)$\triangle AOD \sim \triangle BOC (\triangle AOB \sim \triangle DOC \Rightarrow \frac{AO}{BO}=\frac{DO}{CO}, \angle AOB=\angle DOC)$ \\
    (3)$\triangle PDB \sim \triangle PAC (\angle DPB=\angle APC, \angle PBD=\angle PCA)$ \\
    (4)$\triangle PAD \sim \triangle PCB (\triangle PDB \sim \triangle PAC \Rightarrow \frac{PA}{PC}=\frac{PD}{PB}, \angle APD=\angle CPB)$ \\
    æ ¹æ®ç›¸ä¼¼ï¼Œå¯ä»¥æ¨å‡ºå¦‚ä¸‹ç»“è®ºï¼š \\
    (1)$PAÂ·PB=PDÂ·PC$(å‰²çº¿å®šç†) \\
    (2)$OAÂ·OC=OBÂ·OD$(ç›¸äº¤å¼¦å®šç†) \\
    æ ¹æ®åŒå¼§æ‰€å¯¹çš„åœ†å‘¨è§’ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œè¿˜å¯ä»¥æ¨å‡ºå¦‚ä¸‹ç»“è®ºï¼š\\
    (1)$\angle ADB=\angle ACB$ \\
    (2)$\angle DAC=\angle DBC$ \\
    (3)$\angle BAC=\angle BDC$ \\
\end{model}

\centering
\includegraphics[width=4cm]{picture/828.png}
\caption{å››ç‚¹å…±åœ†å›¾}
\end{figure}
\begin{example}
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œæ­£æ–¹å½¢$ABCD$è¾¹é•¿ä¸º$a$ï¼Œ$E,F$ä¸º$BC,CD$ä¸Šä¸¤åŠ¨ç‚¹ï¼Œä¸”æ»¡è¶³$\angle EAF=45^\circ$ï¼Œè¿$BD$äº¤$AE,AF$äº$M,N$. \\
    (1)å†™å‡ºæ‰€æœ‰ä¸$\triangle AMN$ç›¸ä¼¼çš„ä¸‰è§’å½¢ \\
    (2)æ±‚è¯ï¼š$S_{\triangle AMN}=\frac{1}{2}S_{\triangle AFE}$ \\

    è§£ \\
    (1)$\triangle AMN \sim \triangle DMA \sim \triangle BAN \sim \triangle BME \sim \triangle DFN \sim \triangle AFE$ \\
    åAå­—å‹ï¼š$\triangle AMN \sim \triangle DMA \sim \triangle BAN(\angle MAN=\angle MDA=\angle ABN,\angle AMN=\angle DMA,\angle ANM=\angle BNA)$ \\

    $\triangle AMN\sim\triangle DFN\Rightarrow\frac{AN}{DN}=\frac{MN}{FN}\Rightarrow\frac{AN}{MN}=\frac{ND}{NF},\angle AND=\angle MNF\Rightarrow\triangle AND\sim\triangle MNF\Rightarrow\angle NFM=\angle NDA=45^\circ$ \\
    $\triangle ANE,\triangle AMF$å‡ä¸ºç­‰è…°ç›´è§’ä¸‰è§’å½¢ï¼Œ$\triangle ANE \sim \triangle AMF \Rightarrow \frac{AN}{AM}=\frac{AE}{AF} \Rightarrow \frac{AN}{AE}=\frac{AM}{AF},\angle MAN=\angle FAE\Rightarrow \triangle AMN \sim \triangle AFE$ \\
    è¯æ˜(2) \\
    $\frac{S_{\triangle AMN}}{S_{\triangle AFE}}=\frac{AN^2}{AE^2}=\frac{1}{2}$ \\
    è¯æ˜(3) \\
    $\triangle AFE \sim \triangle AMN \sim \triangle DFN \Rightarrow \angle AFE=\angle DFN$ \\
    $\triangle AFE \sim \triangle AMN \sim \triangle BME \Rightarrow \angle AEF=\angle BEM$ \\

\section{é”è§’çš„ä¸‰è§’æ¯”åŠå…¶æ€§è´¨}
\begin{knowledge}

    (3)$\sin^2 A+\cos^2 A=1$ \\

    (6)$\sin A=\cos(90^\circ-A)$ \\
    (7)$\cos A=\sin(90^\circ-A)$ \\

$\sin A$ & 0 & $\frac{1}{2}$ & $\frac{\sqrt 2}{2}$ & $\frac{\sqrt3}{2}$ & 1 & $\frac{\sqrt 6-\sqrt 2}{4}$ & ... & $\frac{\sqrt 6+\sqrt 2}{4}$\\
\hline
$\cos A$ & 1 & $\frac{\sqrt3}{2}$ & $\frac{\sqrt 2}{2}$ & $\frac{1}{2}$ & 0 & $\frac{\sqrt 6+\sqrt 2}{4}$ & ... & $\frac{\sqrt 6-\sqrt 2}{4}$\\
\hline
$\tan A$ & 0 & $\frac{\sqrt3}{3}$ & 1 & $\sqrt3$ & $\times$ & $2-\sqrt 3 $ & $\sqrt2 - 1$ & $2+\sqrt 3$\\
\hline
$\cot A$ & $\times$ & $\sqrt3$ & 1 & $\frac{\sqrt3}{3}$ & 0 & $2+\sqrt 3 $ & $\sqrt2 + 1$ & $2-\sqrt 3$\\
\hline
\hline
\end{tabular}
\end{table}
\begin{knowledge}
    ç°ç»™å‡ºè®¡ç®—15åº¦è§’ä¸‰è§’æ¯”çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œ22.5åº¦è§’çš„ä¸‰è§’æ¯”å¯ç±»æ¯”æ­¤æ³•æ±‚å¾—ã€‚\\
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œ$\angle A=15^\circ,\angle C=90^\circ$ï¼Œåœ¨$AC$ä¸Šå–ä¸€ç‚¹$D$ï¼Œä½¿å¾—$AD=BD$ï¼Œåˆ™$\angle BDC=30^\circ$ï¼Œè®¾$BC=a$ï¼Œåˆ™$CD=\sqrt3 a,BD=2a,AD=2a,AC=2a+\sqrt3 a,AB=\sqrt{a^2+(2+\sqrt3)^2a^2}=\sqrt{(8+4\sqrt3)a^2}=(\sqrt6+\sqrt2)a$ \\
    $\sin A=\frac{BC}{AB}=\frac{a}{(\sqrt6+\sqrt2)a}=\frac{\sqrt6-\sqrt2}{4}$ \\
    $\cos A=\frac{AC}{AB}=\frac{(2+\sqrt3)a}{(\sqrt6+\sqrt2)a}=\frac{\sqrt6+\sqrt2}{4}$ \\
    $\tan A=\frac{BC}{AC}=\frac{a}{(2+\sqrt3)a}=2-\sqrt3 $ \\
    $\cot A=\frac{AC}{BC}=\frac{(2+\sqrt3)a}{a}=2+\sqrt3 $ \\
\end{knowledge}

\section{*äºŒæ¬¡å‡½æ•°ä¸è§’å¹³åˆ†çº¿}
\begin{model}
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œä¸å¹³è¡Œäº$x$è½´çš„ç›´çº¿$EQF$ä¸æŠ›ç‰©çº¿$y=ax^2$äº¤äº$E,F$ä¸¤ç‚¹ï¼Œåœ¨$y$è½´ä¸Šæ‰¾ä¸€ç‚¹$P$ï¼Œä½¿å¾—$y$è½´å¹³åˆ†$\angle EPF$. \\
    è®¾$E(x_1,y_1),F(x_2,y_2),Q(0,y_3)$ï¼Œåˆ™$P$ç‚¹åæ ‡ä¸º$(0,-y_3)$. \\
    è¯æ˜ï¼šè®¾$P$ç‚¹åæ ‡ä¸º$(0,y_4)$ï¼Œè®¾ç›´çº¿è§£æå¼ä¸º$y=kx+b(k\ne 0)$ï¼Œä¸$y=ax^2$è”ç«‹ï¼Œç”±éŸ¦è¾¾å®šç†å¾—$x_1+x_2=\frac{k}{a},x_1x_2=-\frac{b}{a}$. \\
    $\tan \angle EPQ = -\frac{y_1-y_4}{x_1} = \tan \angle FPQ = \frac{y_2-y_4}{x_2} \Rightarrow x_1y_2+x_2y_1=y_4(x_1+x_2) $ \\
    $x_1(kx_2+b)+x_2(kx_1+b)=y_4(x_1+x_2) \Rightarrow 2kx_1x_2+b(x_1+x_2)=y_4(x_1+x_2)$ \\
    $-\frac{2kb}{a}+\frac{kb}{a}=\frac{k}{a}Â·y_4 \Rightarrow y_4=-b$
\end{model}

\section{å‚å¾„å®šç†}

\section{*åœ†å¹‚å®šç†}
\begin{knowledge}
    åœ†å¹‚å®šç†ï¼šäº¤ç‚¹ä¸º$P$çš„ä¸¤æ¡ç›¸äº¤ç›´çº¿ä¸åœ†$O$ç›¸äº¤äº$A,B$ä¸$C,D$ï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰$PAÂ·PB=PCÂ·PD$ï¼Œè¯æ˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼š$\triangle PAD \sim \triangle PCB$
    æˆ–$\triangle PAC \sim \triangle PDB$. \\

\section{*é˜¿åŸºç±³å¾·æŠ˜å¼¦å®šç†}
\begin{model}
    å¦‚å›¾ï¼Œ$AB,BC$æ˜¯$\bigodot O$ä¸¤æ¡å¼¦ï¼Œ$M$æ˜¯$\mathop{ABC}\limits^{\frown}$çš„ä¸­ç‚¹ï¼Œ$MD\perp BC$ï¼Œå‚è¶³ä¸º$D$ï¼Œæ±‚è¯ï¼š$AB+BD=CD$. \\
    è¯æ˜ï¼šåœ¨$BC$ä¸Šæˆªå–$CG=AB$ï¼Œ$\mathop{AM}\limits^{\frown}=\mathop{MC}\limits^{\frown} \Rightarrow AM=MC$ï¼Œåˆ™$\triangle ABM \backcong \triangle CGM$ï¼Œ
    $MD\perp BC,BM=MG \Rightarrow \triangle BMD \backcong \triangle GMD \Rightarrow BD=DG \Rightarrow AB+BD=CD$.
\end{model}

\centering
\includegraphics[width=4cm]{picture/1104.png}
